<h1 class="h0 mb30">We are <br>the Nation's <br>first line of <br>defense</h1>
<div class="outside-border-left-red mb45-30"><div class="mb60-30">
<p class=""><strong>We accomplish what others cannot accomplish and go where others cannot go</strong></p>
<p class="">A career at CIA is unlike any other. We are looking for people from all backgrounds and walks of life to carry out the work of a Nation.</p>

<h2 class="pt30 col-sm-12 col-md-8 remove-gutters-h">Our Agency </h2>
</div>
<div class="col-sm-12 col-md-6"><div class="overview-content">
<p class=""><strong>We give U.S. leaders the intelligence they need to keep our country safe</strong></p>
<p class="">As the worlds premier foreign intelligence agency, the work we do at CIA is vital to U.S. national security. We collect and analyze foreign intelligence and conduct covert action. U.S. policymakers, including the President of the United States, make policy decisions informed by the information we provide.</p>
<p class=""><a href="about" class="link-button bold" target="_self" rel="noopener noreferrer">Learn About Us</a></p>
</div></div>
</div></div></section><section class="background-grid-black"><div class="container teaser-container"><div class="row align-items-center justify-content-between">
<div class="col-sm-12 col-md-5 order-last teaser-context pv120-90"><div class="content-card-teaser ">
<h2>Our Legacy</h2>
<div class="">
<p class=""><strong>CIAs legacy is one of brave individuals dedicated to freedom, fulfilling our intelligence mission with ingenuity and grit</strong></p>
<p class="">Protecting our country is at the heart of our mission  past, present, and future. From our World War II roots through today, we carry on the traditions of ingenuity, bravery, and quiet sacrifice that have made us the worlds premier foreign intelligence agency.</p>
<a aria-label="Our Legacy" class="button button-default button-black" href="/legacy/"><span class="aria-hiden">Discover Our Legacy</span></a>
</div>
</div></div>
